{"step_index":498,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-04-23T17:44:29Z","content":"The root cause was **Windows line endings (`\\r\\n`)** stored in the database. When the publisher presses Enter in a textarea on Windows, the browser sends `\\r\\n` (carriage return + newline). My earlier code only looked for `\\n\\n` and never found a match, so the entire text was treated as one paragraph.\n\n**What the fix does:**\n1. **Normalize** all `\\r\\n` → `\\n` and `\\r` → `\\n` before any splitting\n2. **Split on double newlines** first (double Enter = paragraph break) \n3. **Fallback to single newlines** if no double newlines are found (single Enter = paragraph break)\n\nYour 5-paragraph article will now render as exactly 5 justified paragraphs. Refresh the article page to confirm!"}

{"step_index":663,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-04-23T18:21:05Z","content":"All the structural fixes are done. Here's what was corrected:\n\n**Root cause:** In Next.js, a `layout.tsx` file cannot pass `props` down to `page.tsx`. My original design had this flaw — the layout was fetching the session and trying to pass `roleName` to the page, which Next.js ignores entirely.\n\n**The fix (proper Next.js pattern):**\n```\npage.tsx        → Server Component (reads session, passes roleName as prop)\n     ↓ renders\nEmployeeAdminClient.tsx  → Client Component ('use client', receives roleName)\n```\n\n**Also fixed:**\n- System Role dropdown now fetches **real roles from the database** instead of hardcoded fake IDs\n- Branches are also fetched live from the database\n- The Audit Log page follows the same server-guard + client-UI pattern\n\n**Please restart the dev server** (`Ctrl+C` then `npm run dev`) to pick up all the new files, then navigate to `/admin/employee` — you should see the new tabbed interface with **Employee List** as the default view."}
